[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `updateName` method in `TarArchiveEntry` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1549[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m1564[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m deserializes [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marbitrary Base64-encoded data from the TAR entry name via [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mObjectInputStream.readObject[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. This uncontrolled deserialization is the direct [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause of the RCE finding.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All TAR parsing and iteration in `TarFile` ultimately invokes this same [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`updateName` logic on every entry. No other parts of the codebase trigger Java [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeserialization.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Critical Logic to Preserve[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All existing header-parsing routines [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`parseTarHeaderUnwrapped`, field [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39massignments, PAX header processing, name normalization[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m must remain unchanged so [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat legitimate archives continue to be handled correctly.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `updateName` hook itself is only invoked in one place [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend of [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`parseTarHeaderUnwrapped`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and only triggers when both `name` and `userName` match [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma very specific pattern. Disabling it will not affect standard archive extraction.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Strategy[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Modify `[0m[1;35mTarArchiveEntry.updateName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString name, String userName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to remove [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe deserialization branch entirely and become a no-op passthrough:[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Change the method body to simply `return name;`.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Retain the method signature and `throws IOException` clause so that callers[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand overrides are unaffected.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Remove now-unused imports related to Base64 decoding and Java serialization:[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `java.util.Base64`[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `java.io.ByteArrayInputStream`[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `java.io.ObjectInputStream`[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `java.lang.ClassNotFoundException`[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Verify that no other code paths rely on this custom deserialization behavior.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Implementation Steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Open [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/tar/TarArchiveEntry.java`.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Locate the `updateName` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m1549[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Replace its entire body with:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        private String [0m[1;35mupdateName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString name, String userName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Disabled deserialization to prevent RCE. Always return the raw name.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            return name;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Remove or clean up the now-unused import statements:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        - import java.util.Base64;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        - import java.io.ByteArrayInputStream;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        - import java.io.ObjectInputStream;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        - import java.lang.ClassNotFoundException;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Rebuild and run the existing test suite to ensure no regressions.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. Rerun the `CompressTarFuzzer` harness to confirm that the RCE finding is [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolved and no new issues have been introduced.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By stubbing out `updateName`, we eliminate the uncontrolled deserialization [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentry point entirely while preserving the remainder of TAR parsing functionality.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The special deserialization behavior [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtriggered only when `name` starts with [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“rO0” and `userName` equals a magic value[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is nonstandard and not required for [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnormal archive processing. Disabling it carries minimal risk of breaking legitimate[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muse cases.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes are made to the fuzzing harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`CompressTarFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m or to [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal dependencies. Existing tests and other archive formats remain unaffected.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigation[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Any clients intentionally using this obscure deserialization-based name [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtransformation will lose that capability. However, this feature poses a severe [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurity risk and was never officially documented, so its removal is warranted.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Removing the imports and code will not affect parsing of valid TAR archives. [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWe recommend adding a short note in the changelog to alert users about the removed [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`updateName` behavior.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After patching, maintainers may choose to implement a safer, whitelisted [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mobject-deserialization mechanism in a future version, but as a first fix, disabling[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe feature fully prevents RCE.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/tar/TarArchiveEntry[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m.jav[0m[1;92ma:1549[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1564[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`CompressTarFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m triggered a high-severity finding [0m[1;39m([0m[39mremote [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode execution[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in `org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.tar.TarArchiveEntry` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhile parsing a malicious TAR header. An attempted patch edited only the import [0m    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe same RCE finding at the same call stack in `TarArchiveEntry.readObject` and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`updateName`.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInitial Issue  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A Jazzer-powered libFuzzer harness fed arbitrary data into `CompressTarFuzzer`, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich reads a TAR stream via `TarFile` and its entries.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- During deserialization in `TarArchiveEntry.updateName`, the fuzzer triggered [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueHigh: Remote Code Execution`. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The stack trace shows unguarded use of Java serialization [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`ObjectInputStream.readObject`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m on externally controlled data in [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mTarArchiveEntry.readObject[0m[1;39m([0m[39m…[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;35mupdateName[0m[1;39m([0m[39m…[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontrolled data” during TAR header parsing.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The vulnerability surfaces in `TarArchiveEntry` constructors invoked by [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TarFile.getNextTarEntry` and ultimately by the fuzz harness.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The harness and instrumentation logs confirm the issue persists across multiple [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
